TextQuestions that need answers! What do you do with your comic books?
Marc Guggenheim: some bagged, rest donated
Peter David: give them out at Halloween
Robert Kirkman: put them away in longboxes
Mike Carey: stack them away
C. B. Cebulski: drop them in longboxes
John Romita Jr.: keep some, give rest away
Bryan Hitch: give them away
Leinil Yu: keep them, extras to friends
Joe Quesada: leave them wherever finished reading for someone else to pick up		?1
